## Project Structure

```sh
└── Repo-Backend/
    ├── .github
    │   └── workflows
    ├── CodigosTest_Backend&Frontend
    │   ├── AuthContext.test.jsx
    │   ├── AuthControllerTest.java
    │   ├── AuthServiceTest.java
    │   ├── JwtExtractorTest.java
    │   ├── JwtServiceTest.java
    │   ├── PrivateRoute.test.jsx
    │   ├── ProjectServiceTest.java
    │   ├── services.test.js
    │   └── vitest.config.js
    ├── README.md
    ├── docker-compose.yml
    ├── innovatech-bff-valdes-munoz
    │   ├── .env
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── node_modules
    │   ├── package-lock.json
    │   ├── package.json
    │   └── src
    ├── kong-gateway
    │   └── kong.yml
    ├── ms-analitica
    │   ├── .mvn
    │   ├── .repomixignore
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── mvnw
    │   ├── mvnw.cmd
    │   ├── pom.xml
    │   ├── src
    │   └── target
    ├── ms-auth
    │   ├── .gitattributes
    │   ├── .gitignore
    │   ├── .mvn
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── mvnw
    │   ├── mvnw.cmd
    │   ├── pom.xml
    │   └── src
    ├── ms-notif
    │   ├── .mvn
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── mvnw
    │   ├── mvnw.cmd
    │   ├── pom.xml
    │   ├── src
    │   └── target
    ├── ms-proyectos
    │   ├── .gitattributes
    │   ├── .gitignore
    │   ├── .mvn
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── mvnw
    │   ├── mvnw.cmd
    │   ├── pom.xml
    │   └── src
    ├── ms-recursos
    │   ├── .mvn
    │   ├── Dockerfile
    │   ├── mvnw
    │   ├── mvnw.cmd
    │   ├── pom.xml
    │   ├── src
    │   └── target
    ├── postman
    │   ├── Innovatech-Backend.postman_collection.json
    │   └── Innovatech-Local.postman_environment.json
    ├── repomix backend.xml
    └── scripts
        └── init-dbs.sql
```

## Getting Started

### Prerequisites

This project requires the following dependencies:

- **Programming Language:** JavaScript
- **Package Manager:** Maven, Npm, Yarn
- **Container Runtime:** Docker

### Installation

Build Repo-Backend from the source and intsall dependencies:

1. **Clone the repository:**

    ```sh
    ❯ git clone https://github.com/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend
    ```

2. **Navigate to the project directory:**

    ```sh
    ❯ cd Repo-Backend
    ```

3. **Install the dependencies:**

<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
    <!-- [![docker][docker-shield]][docker-link] -->
    <!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
    <!-- [docker-shield]: https://img.shields.io/badge/Docker-2CA5E0.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=docker&logoColor=white -->
    <!-- [docker-link]: https://www.docker.com/ -->

    **Using [docker](https://www.docker.com/):**

    ```sh
    ❯ docker build -t Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend .
    ```
<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
    <!-- [![maven][maven-shield]][maven-link] -->
    <!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
    <!-- [maven-shield]: None -->
    <!-- [maven-link]: None -->

    **Using [maven](None):**

    ```sh
    ❯ echo 'INSERT-INSTALL-COMMAND-HERE'
    ```
<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
    <!-- [![npm][npm-shield]][npm-link] -->
    <!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
    <!-- [npm-shield]: https://img.shields.io/badge/npm-CB3837.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=npm&logoColor=white -->
    <!-- [npm-link]: https://www.npmjs.com/ -->

    **Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**

    ```sh
    ❯ npm install
    ```
<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
    <!-- [![yarn][yarn-shield]][yarn-link] -->
    <!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
    <!-- [yarn-shield]: https://img.shields.io/badge/Yarn-2C8EBB.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=yarn&logoColor=white -->
    <!-- [yarn-link]: https://yarnpkg.com/ -->

    **Using [yarn](https://yarnpkg.com/):**

    ```sh
    ❯ yarn install
    ```

### Usage

Run the project with:

**Using [docker](https://www.docker.com/):**
```sh
docker run -it {image_name}
```
**Using [maven](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-RUN-COMMAND-HERE'
```
**Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**
```sh
npm start
```
**Using [yarn](https://yarnpkg.com/):**
```sh
yarn start
```

### Testing

Repo-backend uses the {__test_framework__} test framework. Run the test suite with:

**Using [maven](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-TEST-COMMAND-HERE'
```
**Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**
```sh
npm test
```
**Using [yarn](https://yarnpkg.com/):**
```sh
yarn test
```

## Contributing

- **💬 [Join the Discussions](https://github.com/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **🐛 [Report Issues](https://github.com/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `Repo-Backend` project.
- **💡 [Submit Pull Requests](https://github.com/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your github account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone https://github.com/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to github**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
<summary>Contributor Graph</summary>
<br>
<p align="left">
   <a href="https://github.com{/Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend/}graphs/contributors">
      <img src="https://contrib.rocks/image?repo=Benjvlifts/Repo-Backend">
   </a>
</p>
</details>
